msg:Summary: It is a three-star (minus) hotel, which is too different from the promotional pictures, and lower than Hanting. Partners who usually live in four-star hotels or above should not consider it, they will be very disappointed.
1. Room environment: relatively old, with wooden furniture, small area, and dim lighting. You can see the actual picture for the place that is the most different from the picture. 2023 New Year's Eve Speechless Event
2. The water temperature is not enough: the water temperature for washing in the morning is less than 37 degrees, which is quite cold. Very bad experience in winter.
3. Air conditioner: It is a traditional on-hook, with insufficient heating, and it is really cold in winter. It is too different from the five-star central air-conditioning and floor heating.
4. Restaurant: When I walked into the restaurant, I was shocked. The restaurant of a five-star hotel feels similar to the restaurant of a low-priced tour group. I won't talk about the crowds, after all, it's the Spring Festival. There are less than 10 types of meals, half of which are processed products. The only freshly cooked noodles I was looking forward to was because the chef was extremely inefficient, so I gave up queuing up and visually estimated that it would take 20 minutes to make a base. When we sat down to eat, many of the dining chairs were very dirty, one even looked like it had blood on it?
5. Lobby: It is definitely not the five-star hotel you imagined, but the lobby of a country self-built hotel. The front desk staff also don't have uniforms, they wear their own casual clothes.
The hotel experience is very poor. I won't come again next time. I don't know where so many good reviews come from. Lightning protection.

msg:The hotel is on the edge of the Wuyi Mountain Scenic Area, and is a short distance from the battery station of the bamboo raft wharf.
The hotel room is relatively large and the facilities are outdated, but the service is quite attentive. When you check in, the service staff greets you all the way to the door of the room. The buffet breakfast is not open during special periods, and it will be delivered to the room at the time specified by the guest in the form of a set meal. The timing is very precise, and the variety of breakfast can also be seen with thought.
It's a pity that the only road from the hotel to Sangu Resort is under construction, and there will be traffic jams during the day, with a lot of dust.
In this case, it is a test for tourists to go to Sangu Resort for dining. You can only drive through the hinterland of Wuyi Mountain when the roads in the scenic spot are open at night. Itâ€™s just that the road at night canâ€™t be seen, except for the shaking of trees and the sound of insects, the local cars are flying by with their headlights flashing. Foreign tourists must be bold and careful when going to and from here.
